factor<i></i></span></span>=16.0 <span class="plumedtooltip">TEMP<span class="right">the system temperature - this is only needed if you are doing well-tempered metadynamics<i></i></span></span>=310.0 <span class="plumedtooltip">RESTART<span class="right">allows per-action setting of restart (YES/NO/AUTO)<i></i></span></span>=YES
<span style="display:none;" id="data/tetramer/bias_16/plumed.datmetad">The METAD action with label <b>metad</b> calculates the following quantities:<table  align="center" frame="void" width="95%" cellpadding="5%"><tr><td width="5%"><b> Quantity </b>  </td><td><b> Description </b> </td></tr><tr><td width="5%">metad.bias</td><td>the instantaneous value of the bias potential</td></tr></table></span><span class="plumedtooltip" style="color:green">PRINT<span class="right">Print quantities to a file. <a href="https://www.plumed.org/doc-master/user-doc/html/PRINT" style="color:green">More details</a><i></i></span></span> <span class="plumedtooltip">ARG<span class="right">the labels of the values that you would like to print to the file<i></i></span></span>=<b name="data/tetramer/bias_16/plumed.datrmsda">rmsda</b>,<b name="data/tetramer/bias_16/plumed.datrmsdb">rmsdb</b>,<b name="data/tetramer/bias_16/plumed.datrmsdc">rmsdc</b>,<b name="data/tetramer/bias_16/plumed.datrmsdd">rmsdd</b>,<b name="data/tetramer/bias_16/plumed.datsumrmsdint">sumrmsdint</b>,<b name="data/tetramer/bias_16/plumed.datcmapab">cmapab</b>,<b name="data/tetramer/bias_16/plumed.datcmapbc">cmapbc</b>,<b name="data/tetramer/bias_16/plumed.datcmapcd">cmapcd</b>,<b name="data/tetramer/bias_16/plumed.datrestrainta">restrainta.bias</b>,<b name="data/tetramer/bias_16/plumed.datrestraintb">restraintb.bias</b>,<b name="data/tetramer/bias_16/plumed.datrestraintc">restraintc.bias</b>,<b name="data/tetramer/bias_16/plumed.datmetad">metad.bias</b> <span class="plumedtooltip">FILE<span class="right">the name of the file on which to output these quantities<i></i></span></span>=COLVAR <span class="plumedtooltip">STRIDE<span class="right"> the frequency with which the quantities of interest should be output<i></i></span></span>=100
